--- SrIsahfdayatilakarAmaSArakakftayA bAlapriyAKyawIkayodBAsitayA gosvAmiSrIdAmodaraSAstrinirmitayA vizamasTaladarSanyA vizamasTaladarSinyA divyAYjanAKyawippanyoktayA ca SrImadAcAryABinavaguptaviracitayA locanAKyayA vyAKyayAnugataH /

aTa tatraBavantaH SrImadAcAryABinavaguptapAdAH kAvyAlokavyAKyAnaYcikIrzavastasya nirviGnaparisamAptaye vihitaM samucitezwadevatAnamaskArAtmakammaNgalaM SizyaSiNkzAyE granTatonibaDnantyapUrvamityAdi /

bAlapriyA nA-tattatkAryaM prati prasidDaM yadyadupAdAnAdikAraRantasya kalA leSaH tAM vinA antareREva apUrvaMulokaprasidDavastuvijAtIyamadButaYca vastunirupAKyaSaSaSfNgAdivilakzaRamanamBo 'DikaraRakakamalAdikaM padArTam praTayati sfzwvA vistArayati, kiYca yad grAvapraKyaMupAzARatulyaM nisargato nIrasaM jagatusarvaM vastu nijaH svIyaH kAvyAsambanDI yo rasaH SfNgarAdiH tasya BarAdatiSayAt sArayati sAraM karoti viBAvAditvayojanena rasavyaYjakaM karotIti yAvad, vAkyAByAmAByAM kAvyAtmakasarasvatItattvasya viSvakartuH prajApaterutkarzarUpavyatireko vyaYcitaH; tameva sTirIkartumAha--kramAdityAdi /
yajjagaditi cAnuzajyate, praKyAkaveH pratiBA; upAKyA vacanaM praTamaM praKyA paScAdupAKyeti tayoryaH kramAtprasaraH tena suBagaM hfdyaM sad, BAsayati nisargeRAramaRIyamapi sarvaM vastu rasavyaYjakatvasampadanena rasaRIyaM satprakASayatItyarTaH, cakArasyAtra sambanDaH, atra praKyopAKyAprasarasyApUrvavastunirmARe sarasatvakaraRe ca hetutvamArTikaM boDyam, atrAdyena vAkyenApUrvavastuno nirmARandvitIyena pUrvaM sato vastunassarasatvakaraRaM tftIyena dvayorapi hfdyatayA prakASanaYjoktamityapa vyAcikzate, tatutaTAviDamapUrvavastupraTayitftvAdiDarmaviSizwam, tadDarmasampattyarTamAha-kavIti /
kavisahfdayAvityAKyA yasya tat, kavisahfdayaSabdAvatra nirmARarUpakavivyApAravicArAtmakasahfdayavyApAravizayakAvyaparO, yadvA kavisahfdayErAKyAyatOcyate iti tadAKyam, aTa vA kavisahfdayayorAKyA aBIkzRyena KyAnaM sPuraRaM yasya tat kAvyAtmakamityarTaH, tattvamAropitaM boDyam, sarasvatyAHuSabdaprapaYcABimAninyAdevatAyAH, tattvaMupAramArTikaM rUpam, vijayate sarvasmAdupari vartate, enena tannamaskAro granTakarturgamyate; aTa ca sarasvatyAstattvaM DvanikAvyam, vijayate; apUrvamityAdyarTaH pUrvavadboDya iti pratipAdyArTo 'pyAsUtrita iti dik /
aTOdDatyaM paraharannAtmano vyAKyAnanEpuRI darSayan kIrttya nuvfttaye nAmanirdeSaNkurvaMSca pratijAnIte-BawwetyAdi /

lojyate dfSyate 'neneti locanaM svasya locanaMmanaH tasya nitarAM yojanayA manaHpraRiDAnenetyarTaH, kAvyAlokaM janasya sPuwayAmi visadIkaromi, yadvA svasya locanaM jYAnaM tasya niyojanayA vyAKyAnarUpAnuraRanadvArA samarpaRena sPuwayAmi prakASayAmi, yaTA netrayojanena taTetyupamADvaniratrApi boDyaH /

BaktyA biBarti nEkatvam rUpa-BedAd ayaM DvaniH /

BaktyA biBarti nEkatvaM rUpaBedAdayaM DvaniH ayamuktaprAro DvanirBaktyA nEkatvaM biBarti BinnarUpatvAt /
